###### Our Mission
Our mission is to provide high quality, full lifecycle Electronic Equipment Management Services in a manner that:
  * Ensures the Security of Customer Data,
  * Maximizes the Recovery and Reuse of these Materials,
  * Protects Proprietary Technology, and Delivers Eco-Responsible Solutions


At METech we customize electronics recycling, inventory management and disposal solutions to meet your needs. Electronics recycling is serious business and clients benefit from our transparent tracking and audit processes for commodity recovery and recycling.

# How To Safely Recycle Lithium Batteries
## The World Runs on Batteries
Lithium batteries power everything – including cell phones, laptops, toys, appliances, power tools, and electric toothbrushes. High-tech devices usually contain rechargeable lithium-ion batteries because it is much more convenient to charge a device than it is to frequently dismantle it and replace a standard alkaline disposable battery (commonly used in basic devices like tv remotes or flashlights). Lithium-ion batteries last much longer and have higher power density than traditional batteries.
### What’s in a Lithium Battery?
Lithium batteries are composed of various elements, including lithium-ion or lithium-polymer cells, a protective casing, electrolytes, and valuable metals like cobalt, nickel, and copper. Despite being rechargeable, they will eventually require replacement due to a loss of capacity. You should NOT dispose of them in regular trash or recycling bins, because they contain harmful substances that could be hazardous to the environment if released.
### Types of Lithium Batteries
There are several different types of lithium batteries, each with its own unique composition and applications.
**Lithium Cobalt Oxide (LiCoO2 or LCO)**
This is the most common type of lithium-ion battery and is used in many consumer electronics like laptops, smartphones, and digital cameras. They offer high energy density, providing long-lasting power.
**Lithium Iron Phosphate (LiFePO4 or LFP)**
These batteries are known for their excellent thermal stability and safety characteristics, which is why they are used in devices like electric vehicles, electric bikes, and storage systems for renewable energy. LiFePO4 batteries have a longer cycle life and can withstand high charge and discharge rates.
**Lithium Manganese Oxide (LiMn2O4 or LMO)**
LMO batteries are commonly found in power tools, medical devices, and electric bikes. They can deliver high currents and have a relatively long cycle life.
**Lithium Nickel Manganese Cobalt Oxide (LiNiMnCoO2 or NMC)**
NMC batteries are a popular choice for electric vehicles and energy storage applications. They offer a good balance between high energy density and power output.
**Lithium Nickel Cobalt Aluminum Oxide (LiNiCoAlO2 or NCA)**
NCA batteries are also used in electric vehicles, and have similar advantages to NMC batteries.
**Lithium Titanate (Li4Ti5O12 or LTO)**
LTO batteries are known for their extremely fast charge and discharge rates, which makes them helpful for quick-charging electric buses and energy storage systems. They have a long cycle life and great thermal stability.
### ![](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/06/Lithium_Battery-800.jpg)
### Why is it Important to Recycle Lithium Batteries?
Recycling is critical for conservation of natural resources, minimizing waste, and preventing pollution. By reusing materials from recycled products like valuable metals and minerals, we reduce the need for extracting and processing virgin resources from the earth. This helps conserve natural habitats and minimizes the impact of resource extraction on ecosystems. Recycling lithium batteries also diverts waste from landfills, reducing the rapidly growing need for new landfill sites and keeping harmful substances from entering the environment.
### How Does It Work?
The process of recycling lithium batteries involves several steps to carefully ensure the proper recovery of materials. First, batteries must be separated from regular waste streams. After collection, batteries are sorted based on their types to facilitate efficient processing. The batteries are then dismantled to access the cells inside. Battery cells are the basic building block of a battery that generates electrical energy through chemical reactions. Shredding, sieving, and magnetic separation is then done to sort metallic components from the battery cells. These components undergo further processing to extract valuable metals. Remaining components, including plastics, are then disposed of responsibly.
### Dangers of Improper Lithium Battery Disposal
Lithium batteries contain a sheet that separates electrodes and prevents short-circuiting. If a battery is crushed or punctured in any way, the separator could be breached causing a thermal reaction – leading to a spark or fire. If the compromised battery is near any flammable material or there are a bunch of batteries together (say in a landfill or a recycling center) it could be a recipe for disaster. In recent years, there have been many [lithium ion battery fires](https://www.cnn.com/2023/03/09/tech/lithium-ion-battery-fires/index.html) due to malfunction or improper handling.
Lithium is highly reactive: temperature, charging voltage, and casing damage can cause a thermal reaction. That’s why airline passengers are recommended to keep laptops and cell phones in their carry-on bags, and [prohibited from checking spare lithium batteries and e-cigarettes in luggage](https://www.faa.gov/newsroom/lithium-batteries-baggage#:~:text=Spare%20\(uninstalled\)%20lithium%20metal%20batteries,passenger%20in%20carry%2Don%20baggage.). Proper handling is ALWAYS required to prevent fire and pollution risk while recycling lithium batteries.
### Electronics Recycling at METech
We offer end-to-end [IT Asset Disposition and Data Security services](https://www.metechrecycling.com/services/) for government, healthcare, and technology clients across the United States. We are continuously improving our processes and implementing the latest technologies to provide the safest and most sustainable ITAD in the world. [Contact an expert at METech](https://www.metechrecycling.com/contact-us/) to learn how we can design a customized solution for your organization today.
[admin](https://www.metechrecycling.com/author/admin/ "Posts by admin")2025-07-09T12:38:33+00:00June 30, 2023|

# Solar BESS Decommissioning: Safety, Compliance, and Recycling
As solar projects continue to scale across utility, commercial, and community environments, Battery Energy Storage Systems (BESS) have become an essential component of modern [solar infrastructure.](https://www.metechrecycling.com/solar-panel-recycling/) By storing excess generation for use at peak demand, BESS technology increases system resilience, improves grid stability, and maximizes solar ROI.
But just like PV panels and inverters, a BESS eventually reaches the end of its usable life. Whether due to capacity degradation, safety concerns, or system upgrades, **proper end-of-life planning is crucial for solar developers, EPCs, asset owners, and O &M teams.**
[METech Recycling](https://www.metechrecycling.com/) specializes in safe, compliant, and sustainable BESS decommissioning for solar sites of any scale.
* * *
## **1. Why BESS End-of-Life Planning Matters for Solar Projects**
A BESS is composed of battery modules, inverters, thermal management systems, wiring, and enclosures—all of which require careful handling at end-of-life.
For solar operators, failure to plan ahead can lead to:
  * **Safety risks** from high-voltage lithium-ion components
  * **Fire hazards** associated with thermal runaway
  * **Regulatory non-compliance** during hazardous-material transport
  * **Environmental impact** from improper disposal of lithium, cobalt, and nickel
  * **Lost revenue** by overlooking second-life or material recovery opportunities


Integrating BESS decommissioning into the solar lifecycle protects your project, your personnel, and your investment.
* * *
## **2. The BESS Decommissioning Process for Solar Sites**
METech simplifies the technical, regulatory, and logistical challenges involved in retiring energy storage systems from solar farms.
### **a. Planning & Risk Assessment**
  * Document system capacity (MW/MWh), site layout, and component details
  * Create a solar-specific Decommissioning Plan
  * Conduct hazard assessments
  * Ensure compliance with EPA, DOT, and local AHJ rules
  * Prepare chain-of-custody documentation


### **b. De-Energize & Disconnect**
  * Safely discharge and electrically isolate all battery units
  * Disconnect DC-coupled or AC-coupled solar tie-ins
  * Follow strict LOTO (lock-out/tag-out) procedures


### **c. Removal & Transport**
  * Dismantle racks, containers, and wiring
  * Package lithium batteries to Class 9 hazmat standards
  * Coordinate nationwide transport to METech’s R2v3-certified facilities


### **d. Second-Life Evaluation & Recycling**
  * Test modules for remaining capacity (possible use: microgrids, backup storage)
  * Recycle non-viable modules to recover lithium, cobalt, nickel, and copper
  * Process auxiliary solar equipment such as inverters, transformers, and BOS gear


### **e. Site Restoration**
  * Remove remaining structures and storage enclosures
  * Clear concrete or metal foundations as required
  * Provide full reporting for environmental and ESG documentation


* * *
## **3. Second Life vs. Recycling for Solar BESS**
### **Second Life Applications**
Battery modules with usable capacity can be repurposed into:
  * Backup systems for ag facilities
  * Community microgrids
  * Off-grid storage for low-demand sites


This supports both sustainability and cost efficiency in the solar ecosystem.
### **Responsible Recycling**
When reuse isn’t viable, METech ensures:
  * Full recovery of metals (lithium, cobalt, nickel, copper)
  * Proper processing of plastics, wiring, and metals
  * Zero landfill for hazardous components


Our R2v3-certified processes ensure all materials are handled safely and responsibly.
* * *
## **4. Compliance Requirements for Solar BESS**
End-of-life energy storage is regulated under multiple frameworks, including:
  * **EPA hazardous waste regulations**
  * **DOT hazmat transport rules**
  * **Fire code requirements (NFPA 855, IFC)**
  * **Local environmental permits**
  * **ESG and sustainability reporting for investors**
  * **Decommissioning bonds and closure plans for utility-scale assets**


Working with a certified recycling partner keeps solar operators fully compliant from removal to material recovery.
* * *
## **5. Why Solar Developers Choose METech Recycling**
With over 50 years of industry experience and deep solar-sector expertise, METech offers:
  * **Turnkey BESS decommissioning** from planning to final recycling
  * **Specialized handling of lithium-ion systems** and energy-storage hazards
  * **R2v3-certified recycling** for batteries, inverters, wiring, and BOS components
  * **Nationwide logistics capabilities** for utility-scale solar sites
  * **Detailed chain-of-custody and destruction documentation**
  * **ESG-aligned reporting** for sustainability metrics
  * **A minority-owned, inclusive organization committed to environmental stewardship**


Whether your project is 5 MW or 500 MW, METech ensures a safe, efficient, and compliant lifecycle closure.
* * *
## **6. Take the Next Step: Plan Your Solar BESS Decommissioning**
End-of-life doesn’t have to mean end of value.
METech helps solar developers, EPCs, and asset owners:
  * Assess system condition and recycling options
  * Estimate decommissioning cost and recovery potential
  * Build compliant end-of-life programs
  * Create documentation for permitting and ESG reporting


[**Contact us today**](https://www.metechrecycling.com/contact-us/) to learn how we can help on your current solar project.

## [How To Safely Recycle Lithium Batteries](https://www.metechrecycling.com/2023/06/30/how-to-safely-recycle-lithium-batteries/)
The World Runs on Batteries Lithium batteries power everything - including cell phones, laptops, toys, appliances, power tools, and electric toothbrushes. High-tech devices usually contain rechargeable lithium-ion batteries because it is much more convenient to charge a device than it is to frequently dismantle it and replace a standard alkaline disposable battery (commonly used in basic devices like tv remotes or flashlights). Lithium-ion batteries last much longer and have higher power density than traditional batteries. What’s in a Lithium Battery? Lithium batteries are composed of various elements, including lithium-ion or lithium-polymer cells, a protective casing, electrolytes, and valuable metals [...]

## [Solar BESS Decommissioning: Safety, Compliance, and Recycling](https://www.metechrecycling.com/2025/11/20/solar-bess-battery-energy-storage-system-recycling/)
As solar projects continue to scale across utility, commercial, and community environments, Battery Energy Storage Systems (BESS) have become an essential component of modern solar infrastructure. By storing excess generation for use at peak demand, BESS technology increases system resilience, improves grid stability, and maximizes solar ROI. But just like PV panels and inverters, a BESS eventually reaches the end of its usable life. Whether due to capacity degradation, safety concerns, or system upgrades, proper end-of-life planning is crucial for solar developers, EPCs, asset owners, and O&M teams. METech Recycling specializes in safe, compliant, and sustainable BESS decommissioning for solar [...]

## [Closing the Loop on Renewable Energy: METech at RE+ 2025](https://www.metechrecycling.com/2025/08/18/metech-re-plus-2025/)
The renewable energy industry is growing at record speed—but with every new innovation comes a responsibility: what happens when clean technology reaches the end of its life? From solar panels and wind components to EV batteries and the data centers that power renewable infrastructure, today’s breakthrough technologies will eventually require safe, responsible recycling. Without sustainable solutions, this waste risks piling up in landfills, creating new challenges for the very industry working to reduce our environmental impact. At METech Recycling, we’ve been preparing for this moment for more than 50 years. As an R2v3-certified recycler, we help renewable energy companies manage [...]

## [What Happens When Solar Panels Are Thrown Away?](https://www.metechrecycling.com/2025/07/10/what-happens-when-solar-panels-are-thrown-away/)
The solar industry is booming. Across rooftops, deserts, and fields, panels are being installed at record pace to meet ambitious renewable energy goals. But there’s a challenge the industry is only beginning to face: what happens when these panels stop producing power? Solar panels typically last 20–30 years, meaning the first generation of large-scale installations is already approaching retirement. By the 2030s, millions of tons of solar panels will reach end-of-life each year. Without a plan, many of them risk ending up in landfills or being processed by unregulated facilities that don’t properly handle the materials inside. This is the [...]

The scarcity of rare earth metals and environmental impact of the mining process poses an increasingly urgent question - can rare earth metals be recycled? What are Rare Earth Metals? # Careers
#### [ENGINEER I](https://www.metechrecycling.com/careers/#823baf9716eb1f3c7)
Metech Recycling Inc. is currently seeking to fill the position of Engineer I located in Gilroy, CA. The position is primarily responsible for handling all aspects of the mechanical engineering function. This includes but not limited to design, construction, and installation of equipment modifications, providing technical support to the operating facility, and recommending areas of improvement.  
Essential job duties include:
  * Work closely with Environmental and Safety teams to ensure compliance is implemented into new projects.
  * Responsible for designing, installing and commissioning product units, monitoring modifications and upgrades, and troubleshooting existing processes.
  * Ensure implemented processes work at the optimum level, to the right rate and quality of output, in order to meet supply needs.
  * Maintenance of equipment covering all phases of heavy industrial plant engineering, typical of the metals industry.
  * Optimize equipment utilization and efficiency by applying the latest development in machine procedures, diagnostic equipment, and more reliable electrical components.
  * Develop practical solutions to repetitive equipment failure problems that contribute to the effectiveness of the maintenance effort.
  * Contribute engineering expertise to project work and selection of replacement or new equipment to help ensure consistency and standardization of components and ease of maintenance.
  * Ensure all equipment recommended, repaired or modified meets all company and governmental safety and health rules and regulations to help ensure safety and wellbeing of employees.
  * Assist in the development of engineering or maintenance procedures and repair work to ensure they are safe, effective and efficient. Expand, continually, knowledge of engineering and maintenance principals and practice.
  * Responsible for conducting process development experiments when necessary prior to implementation.
  * Responsible for collecting and interpreting data from the other technical and operating staff involved in the implementation and operations of new equipment and processes.
  * Develops and maintains control charts and monitoring systems to ensure that variances in process are handled and do not affect product quality or recovery.
  * Support the implementation and maintenance of a Quality System by serving as a resource to Operating Teams.


**Requirements** :
Bachelor degree in Mechanical engineering or a related field. At least 2 years of experience in mechanical engineering or related fields. Experienced working in an industrial setting and able to read engineer drawings. Must have knowledge of manufacturing processes, feasibility testing, engineering design, operations and perform equipment, data analysis techniques such as SPC. Must have experience in imaging analysis methodologies and applications. Must have solid computer skills with software application proficiency, including Microsoft office, CAD, 3DMAX and MAYA. Must be motivated, self-starter with a desire to improve production reliability, and have ability to clearly communicate effectively with all levels of the company. Please forward your resume and cover letter to Rex Cheng, rcheng@metechrecycling.com. Refer to the position of Engineer I.
METech is an EOE.
#### [CUSTOMER SERVICE REPRESENTATIVE](https://www.metechrecycling.com/careers/#8b4a967b425c9ff00)
Job Title: Customer Service Representative
Pay: $19.00 per hour
Reports To: Assistant Director of Operations
Location: Gilroy, CA
**GENERAL DUTIES:**
  1. Receives customers’ requests by telephone or email, analyzes requests, provides information requested or ascertains who can best provide the information, and routes the request to the proper person.
  2. Schedules shipping to Metech for customers.
  3. Analyzes transactions, corrects records, and adjusts errors.
  4. Maintains appropriate files and records, both electronic and paper in accordance with Metech policies and procedures as a resource for the sales force and provide references helpful to the customer. Prepares customer-specific reports.
  5. Opens customer accounts by recording account information.
  6. Maintains the material pickup schedule and coordinates with the driver and the customer to assure satisfactory conduct of the operations and to assist the customer.
  7. Resolves customer questions related to orders, takes orders as needed, recommends or selects the best method to solve problems, expediting the correction or adjustment, and follows up to ensure the satisfactory resolution.
  8. Maintains liaison with other departments for order completion.
  9. Prepares customer invoice, acknowledgement of receipts for materials and certificates of destruction and ensures that they are routed or mailed.
  10. Responds to customers’ requests via telephone or mail, using personal computer when necessary.
  11. Applies knowledge of Metech policies and procedures for pickup and processing materials, the commitments made by Metech for responsible recycling, unacceptable items and the pricing of services.
  12. Assists in completing or routing customer requests for environmental audits or other regulatory information to satisfy contract or proposal requirements. Assists with proposal routing and related correspondence. Provides certificate of insurance.
  13. Prepares receiving reports by collecting and analyzing customer information.
  14. Contributes to a team effort by accomplishing related tasks as needed.
  15. Assists with event planning and logistics including occasional onsite participation in marketing events, collection events and conventions or meetings.


**ADDITIONAL ADMIN RESPONSIBILITIES:**
  1. Provides switchboard relief as needed.
  2. May assist with coordination, arrangements, and actual conduct of collection events.
  3. Performs other allied duties as assigned by supervisor.


**CONDUCT:** To perform the job successfully, employees should demonstrate the following:
  * **Organizational Support:** Follow policies and procedures; complete administrative tasks correctly and on time; support organization’s goals and values.
  * **Quality:** Demonstrate accuracy and thoroughness; look for ways to improve and promote quality; apply feedback to improve performance; monitor own work to ensure quality.
  * **Quantity:** Meet productivity standards; complete work in timely manner; strive to increase productivity; work quickly.
  * **Dependability:** Follow instructions, respond to management direction; take responsibility for own actions; keep commitments; work overtime and possible weekends when necessary to meet goals; complete tasks on time, or request alternate plan from Supervisor or Operations Manager.


**EXPERIENCE AND BACKGROUND:**
One (1) year of experience in customer service or sales, preferably for a service industry is desired. Knowledge of recycling industry standards and practices strongly desired. Knowledge of graphic arts, website maintenance, and general advertising principals and techniques is desired. Experience with operations in an ISO 9001 and/or 14001 environment is preferable.
**EDUCATION:**
High school education or equivalent. Some post-diploma training in business principals or an Associate degree in a related field is desired.
**Language Skills:** Ability to compose, read, and comprehend instructions, memorandums, business correspondence, and reports in English. Ability to effectively present information in one-on-one and small group situations to customers, vendors, and employees within the organization. Strong written and verbal communication skills are essential.
**Reasoning Ability:** Ability to apply common sense understanding to carry out instructions furnished in written, oral, or diagram form. Ability to deal with problems involving several concrete variables in standardized situations.
**Competency :** To perform the job successfully, an individual should demonstrate the following competencies.
  * **Change Management** – Develops workable implementation plans; communicates changes effectively; builds commitment and overcomes resistance; prepares and supports those affected by change; monitors transition, and evaluates results.
  * **Leadership** – Exhibits confidence in self and others; inspires and motivates others to perform well; effectively influences actions and opinions of others; accepts feedback from others; gives appropriate recognition to others.
  * **Cost Consciousness** – works within approved budget; develops and implements cost saving measures; contributes to profits and revenue; conserves organizational resources.
  * **Ethics** – Treats people with respect; keeps commitments; inspires the trust of others; works with integrity; upholds organizational values.
  * **Organizational Support** – Follows policies and procedures; completes administrative tasks correctly and on time; supports organization’s goals and values; benefits organization through outside activities.


**Computer Skills:** Proficiency in electronic mail communications, MS Office including MS Word, Excel, and PowerPoint required.
**Other Skills and Abilities:** Must possess good interpersonal skills and have the ability to develop and maintain solid working relationships with warehouse, office, and field personnel. Ability to add, subtract, multiply, and divide in all units of measure, using whole numbers, measure.
Must be willing to conduct independent overnight travel as needed to complete off-site visits. Travel may include aircraft and ground transportation and hotel accommodations.
**Certificates, Licenses, Registrations:** Must possess current government issued drivers license.
**Physical Demands:** While performing the duties of this job, the employee is regularly required to use hands to handle or feel. The employee is frequently required to stand; reach with hands and arms, and talk or hear. The employee is occasionally required to walk, sit, climb, balance, stoop, or kneel. The employee must occasionally lift and/or move up to 30 pounds. Specific vision abilities required by this job include close vision, color vision, peripheral vision, and depth perception and ability to adjust focus.
**Work Environment:** The work environment characteristics described here are representative of those an employee encounters while performing the essential functions of this job. Reasonable accommodations may be made to enable individuals with disabilities to perform the essential functions.
**Note:**
This description although intended to be an accurate depiction of the job, does not necessarily reflect an exhaustive list of responsibilities, requirements, working conditions etc. It may be revised by the employer when circumstances change (e.g. work load, changes in equipment/procedure, staffing changes).

## [Solar BESS Decommissioning: Safety, Compliance, and Recycling](https://www.metechrecycling.com/2025/11/20/solar-bess-battery-energy-storage-system-recycling/)
As solar projects continue to scale across utility, commercial, and community environments, Battery Energy Storage Systems (BESS) have become an essential component of modern solar infrastructure. By storing excess generation for use at peak demand, BESS technology increases system resilience, improves grid stability, and maximizes solar ROI. But just like PV panels and inverters, a BESS eventually reaches the end of its usable life. Whether due to capacity degradation, safety concerns, or system upgrades, proper end-of-life planning is crucial for solar developers, EPCs, asset owners, and O&M teams. METech Recycling specializes in safe, compliant, and sustainable BESS decommissioning for solar [...]

## [How To Safely Recycle Lithium Batteries](https://www.metechrecycling.com/2023/06/30/how-to-safely-recycle-lithium-batteries/)
The World Runs on Batteries Lithium batteries power everything - including cell phones, laptops, toys, appliances, power tools, and electric toothbrushes. High-tech devices usually contain rechargeable lithium-ion batteries because it is much more convenient to charge a device than it is to frequently dismantle it and replace a standard alkaline disposable battery (commonly used in basic devices like tv remotes or flashlights). Lithium-ion batteries last much longer and have higher power density than traditional batteries. What’s in a Lithium Battery? Lithium batteries are composed of various elements, including lithium-ion or lithium-polymer cells, a protective casing, electrolytes, and valuable metals [...]

## [Solar BESS Decommissioning: Safety, Compliance, and Recycling](https://www.metechrecycling.com/2025/11/20/solar-bess-battery-energy-storage-system-recycling/)
As solar projects continue to scale across utility, commercial, and community environments, Battery Energy Storage Systems (BESS) have become an essential component of modern solar infrastructure. By storing excess generation for use at peak demand, BESS technology increases system resilience, improves grid stability, and maximizes solar ROI. But just like PV panels and inverters, a BESS eventually reaches the end of its usable life. Whether due to capacity degradation, safety concerns, or system upgrades, proper end-of-life planning is crucial for solar developers, EPCs, asset owners, and O&M teams. ## [What Happens When Solar Panels Are Thrown Away?](https://www.metechrecycling.com/2025/07/10/what-happens-when-solar-panels-are-thrown-away/)
The solar industry is booming. Across rooftops, deserts, and fields, panels are being installed at record pace to meet ambitious renewable energy goals. But there’s a challenge the industry is only beginning to face: what happens when these panels stop producing power? Solar panels typically last 20–30 years, meaning the first generation of large-scale installations is already approaching retirement. By the 2030s, millions of tons of solar panels will reach end-of-life each year. Without a plan, many of them risk ending up in landfills or being processed by unregulated facilities that don’t properly handle the materials inside. This is the [...]
[Natalka Fydyshyn](https://www.metechrecycling.com/author/natalka/ "Posts by Natalka Fydyshyn")2025-08-19T00:03:42+00:00July 10, 2025|

## [Solar Panel Recycling Companies Leading the Way to a Greener Future](https://www.metechrecycling.com/2023/08/07/solar-panel-recycling-companies-leading-the-way-to-a-greener-future/)
Responsible Recycling for Renewable Energy Sources is Critical Solar panel recycling companies like METech Recycling are invested in a greener future through renewable energy sources. Solar energy plays a pivotal role in the combat against climate change as we move away from fossil fuels. According to a study by the U.S Department of Energy, 40% of the nation’s electricity has the potential to be powered by solar energy by 2035. However, as the number of decommissioned solar panels grow, recyclers, businesses, and consumers must step up to ensure that they are properly disposed of. How Do Solar Panels [...]

Certified Data Destruction[admin](https://www.metechrecycling.com/author/admin/ "Posts by admin")2025-05-07T13:29:35+00:00
# Certified Data Destruction
**Protect Your Data with Certified Data Destruction**
[![Certified Data Destruction - R2v3 Certified](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/11/R2-Stacked-300x185.png)](https://sustainableelectronics.org/)
Certified Data Destruction – R2v3 Certified
In today’s digital world, data security is paramount. At Metech Recycling, we provide Certified Data Destruction services that ensure your sensitive information is permanently and securely erased. Our **R2v3-certified** process guarantees compliance with industry-leading security and environmental standards, giving you the peace of mind that your data is handled with the highest level of integrity.
**METech Recycling Secure Data Destruction Services**
  * **Secure Certified Physical Destruction** – METech physically destroys hard drives, solid-state drives, and other storage media, rendering data completely irretrievable.
  * **Certified Software Data Eradication** – Our advanced software-based data wiping methods ensure that digital information is securely removed and totally unrecoverable.
  * **R2v3 Certified Compliance** – As an **R2v3-certified** facility, METech adheres to the highest standards in responsible recycling and data security. We meet the strictest regulatory and environmental requirements in the industry.


### **Multi-Layered Data Erasure Options**
We offer multiple levels of software-based data erasure—from single-pass to seven-pass—designed to meet the strictest industry standards. Our services comply with:
  * NIST standards
  * Department of Defense standards
  * ITAR registered
  * HIPAA compliant
  * R2v3 data handling protocols


### **In-House Physical Destruction**
When devices cannot be erased through software, we physically destroy them onsite using industrial shredders. This is essential for non-functioning hard drives or proprietary equipment. METech is one of the few electronics recyclers with in-house shredding capacity, ensuring added security and speed.
### **Compliance-Ready Documentation**
Each job includes:
  * Certificates of Data Destruction
  * Chain-of-custody logs
  * Compliance summaries


These documents are available via our secure client portal and are formatted to support audits, legal compliance, and internal governance protocols.
**Why Choose Metech Recycling?**
✔ **Guaranteed Data Security** – We provide **detailed certificates of destruction** for compliance and audit purposes.  
✔ **Eco-Friendly & Responsible** – Our processes align with responsible recycling practices to reduce environmental impact.  
✔ **Trusted by Businesses & Government Agencies** – We serve corporations, healthcare institutions, financial organizations, and government agencies nationwide.
**Get Started Today!**
Ensure your data is permanently erased and disposed of responsibly. Contact **Metech Recycling** today to [schedule a consultation or request a quote](https://www.metechrecycling.com/contact-us/).
## Delivering Eco-Responsible Solutions
![Metech Recycling](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Metech-Footer-Logo.png)
METech Recycling holds the required R2v3 certification in addition to other voluntary certifications allowing us to complete the Circle of Excellence assuring best practices in electronics recycling.

Data Center Recycling Solutions[admin](https://www.metechrecycling.com/author/admin/ "Posts by admin")2025-06-17T17:54:16+00:00
# **Data Center Recycling Solutions**
**Data Center Recycling Solutions and Decommissioning Services by METech Recycling**
METech Recycling offers end-to-end data center recycling solutions and decommissioning services designed to ensure secure, compliant, and environmentally responsible handling of IT infrastructure. Our comprehensive approach minimizes downtime, mitigates risk, and maximizes value recovery for our clients.
**Key Services Include:**
  * **Asset Inventory and Evaluation:** Comprehensive cataloging and assessment of all data center equipment, including servers, storage devices, networking equipment, and peripherals.
  * **Secure Data Erasure and Destruction:** Certified processes for erasing or destroying sensitive data in compliance with industry standards, including NIST 800-88 and ITAR regulations.
  * **Equipment Removal and Logistics:** Safe dismantling, packaging, and transport of equipment, with secure chain-of-custody tracking.
  * **Recycling and Reclamation:** Environmentally responsible recycling of obsolete hardware, ensuring compliance with zero-landfill policies and resource recovery initiatives.
  * **IT Asset Disposition (ITAD):** Reuse, resale, or donation of valuable assets to maximize returns and reduce waste.
  * **Detailed Reporting and Certification:** Documentation of all processes, including data destruction certificates, recycling summaries, and compliance records for auditing purposes.


**Pre-Project:**
  * Thoroughly review the Scope of Work.
  * Assign dedicated team to manage project.
  * Outline the specific tasks and activities involved.
  * Detail hardware removal, data sanitization, and facility cleanup.
  * Establish Project Timeline
  * Display a timeline or Gantt chart showing key milestones and deadlines.
  * Highlight the estimated duration of the decommissioning process.
  * Manage communication with relevant stakeholders.
  * Include contact information for project leads and points of contact.


**Active Onsite:**
  * Data Backup and Migration:
  * Power Down and Disconnect:
  * Cable Management:
  * Dismantling Equipment:
  * Audit and Serial Number Capture
  * Data Destruction:
  * Hardware Handling and packaging
  * Cleaning and Site Restoration


**Post-Project:**
  * Secure Transport to our “in house” processing Facility maintaining full chain of custody.
  * Transfer records into Cloud -based Client Portal for Inventory Management and Record Archiving
  * Material Evaluation
  * Secure Data Erasure
  * Testing & Refurb
  * Parts Harvesting
  * Remarketing
  * Environmentally Responsible Recycling
  * Data Destruction Certificates
  * Redeployment if needed
  * Financial Reconciliation
  * Client or Stakeholder Debriefing


**Highest Return on Asset Value**
  * Test, Refurbish, and Configuration to ensure Top Value
  * Bulk packaging to enhance value
  * Ability to Utilize Multiple Sales Platforms
  * Global Buyers and Partners allow flexibility to Capitalize on Global Market Demand
  * Experience and Reputation
  * Digital reporting


With a proven track record in managing complex data center recycling solutions and projects for enterprise companies, METech Recycling ensures a seamless decommissioning process that aligns with your compliance, security, and sustainability goals.
![R2 V3 Certified](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/11/R2-Stacked-300x185.png)

![Data Center Solutions](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/04/Data-Center-Solutions.png)
Data Center Solutions[admin](https://www.metechrecycling.com/author/admin/ "Posts by admin")2025-07-07T15:58:33+00:00
# **Data Center Solutions**
## Scalable Decommissioning, Auditing, and Lifecycle Management
At METech Recycling, we specialize in **Data Center Solutions** that are tailored to meet the complex demands of today’s data-driven infrastructure. Data center managers face constant pressure—from growing hardware inventories and compliance regulations to sustainability goals and the need for secure asset disposition. Our scalable, turnkey services are designed to help you manage these challenges with confidence, minimize downtime, protect sensitive data, and optimize return on investment.
### Onsite and Remote Decommissioning
Whether you’re closing down a server room or transitioning an entire data center floor, METech provides comprehensive decommissioning services both onsite and remotely. Our trained technicians manage every step of the process, including:
  * Safe removal of racks, servers, and cabling
  * Organized cable management and dismantling
  * Systematic labeling and asset cataloging
  * Secure transport to our certified processing facilities


We ensure that every asset is handled with care and according to best practices, reducing risk while increasing operational efficiency.
### Asset Recovery and Redeployment
As part of our full-service approach to **Data Center Solutions** , we test and refurbish recoverable hardware—such as servers, switches, storage arrays, and other high-value equipment. These assets can be securely redeployed within your network or resold through vetted remarketing channels. All data is sanitized according to Department of Defense (DoD) and NIST 800-88 standards, ensuring total data security and regulatory compliance.
### Real-Time Chain of Custody and Auditing
We provide a fully documented, real-time chain of custody from point of pickup to final disposition. Each asset is tracked using barcode scanning and live inventory systems, giving your team peace of mind and audit-readiness at every stage.
### Environmental Compliance and Certifications
With **[R2v3](https://sustainableelectronics.org/), ISO 9001:2015, ISO 14001:2015, ISO 45001:2018 certifications**, METech ensures your retired equipment is processed with the highest environmental and ethical standards in the industry.
### Custom Data Center Solutions Audit Support for Compliance
Our Data Center Solutions include detailed compliance reporting for your records, including:
  * Energy savings and carbon offset data
  * Hazardous materials tracking
  * Asset retirement certificates


Partner with METech for secure, sustainable, and cost-effective data center lifecycle management. [Contact us today!](https://www.metechrecycling.com/contact-us/)
## Delivering Eco-Responsible Solutions
![Metech Recycling](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Metech-Footer-Logo.png)
METech Recycling holds the required R2v3 certification in addition to other voluntary certifications allowing us to complete the Circle of Excellence assuring best practices in electronics recycling.

Data Security[admin](https://www.metechrecycling.com/author/admin/ "Posts by admin")2025-07-09T13:25:23+00:00
# CCompliant Data Security
### **Data Protection That Goes Beyond Compliance**
Protecting your organization’s sensitive information is at the heart of our operations. As data privacy regulations grow more complex, we ensure you stay ahead of the curve with our best-in-class data destruction services.
### **Multi-Layered Data Erasure Options**
We offer multiple levels of software-based data erasure—from single-pass to seven-pass—designed to meet the strictest industry standards. Our services comply with:
  * NIST standards
  * Department of Defense standards
  * ITAR registered
  * HIPAA compliant
  * R2v3 data handling protocols


Every data-bearing device is tracked from arrival to final disposition through our inventory system, and is assigned a unique identifier to ensure full chain-of-custody compliance.
### **In-House Physical Destruction**
When devices cannot be erased through software, we physically destroy them onsite using industrial shredders. This is essential for non-functioning hard drives or proprietary equipment. METech is one of the few electronics recyclers with in-house shredding capacity, ensuring added security and speed.
### **Compliance-Ready Documentation**
Each job includes:
  * Certificates of Data Destruction
  * Chain-of-custody logs
  * Compliance summaries


These documents are available via our secure client portal and are formatted to support audits, legal compliance, and internal governance protocols.
**Protecting Privacy, Securing Peace of Mind**
## Delivering Eco-Responsible Solutions
![Metech Recycling](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Metech-Footer-Logo.png)
METech Recycling holds the required R2v3 certification in addition to other voluntary certifications allowing us to complete the Circle of Excellence assuring best practices in electronics recycling.

Defense and Government Recycling[admin](https://www.metechrecycling.com/author/admin/ "Posts by admin")2025-07-07T16:00:59+00:00
# Defense and Government Electronic Recycling
### **Protecting National Security and Meeting Compliance with Secure Defense and Government Electronic Recycling**
In sectors like defense, government, and higher education, the secure disposal of outdated or end-of-life electronics is a critical responsibility. At METech Recycling, we specialize in Defense and Government Electronic Recycling solutions designed to meet the stringent requirements of these industries, including sensitive data protection, compliance with federal regulations, and environmentally responsible disposal.
As an **ITAR-registered** and **minority business supplier** , METech Recycling is uniquely positioned to address the complex needs of government agencies, military operations, and educational institutions, ensuring your organization’s electronics are processed securely, sustainably, and in full compliance with all regulatory standards.
### **Why Choose Secure Electronics Recycling?**
Sensitive data on electronics, such as computers, servers, and mobile devices, must be handled with the utmost care. Choosing **Metech Recycling** means:
  * **Data Security**
    * Our **certified data destruction services** ensure the permanent and secure elimination of sensitive and classified information from electronics.
    * Options include physical destruction (e.g., hard drive shredding) or certified data wiping, tailored to meet specific security protocols.
  * **Regulatory Compliance**
    * METech adheres to strict standards, including: 
      * Department of Defense (DoD) data destruction guidelines.
      * NIST 800-88 Media Sanitization standards.
      * ITAR compliance for defense-related materials.
    * We ensure compliance with all local, state, and federal electronic waste regulations, so your organization avoids risk and liability.
  * **Tailored Solutions**
    * We provide customized services designed to meet the unique requirements of defense, government, and education sectors, including: 
      * On-site or off-site data destruction.
      * Comprehensive tracking and documentation for full chain-of-custody transparency.
      * Logistics support for secure transport of sensitive materials.
  * **Environmental Responsibility**
    * Our R2v3, ISO 9001:2015, ISO 14001:2015, ISO 45001:2018-certified processes focus on recovering valuable materials, reducing waste, and supporting a **zero-landfill policy**.
    * Partnering with METech demonstrates a strong commitment to sustainability and compliance with federal green initiatives.


### **Eco-Friendly Disposal Solutions for Defense and Government Electronic Recycling**
We securely process a wide range of electronic devices, including:
  * Computers, laptops, and servers.
  * Mobile devices, printers, and scanners.
  * Networking and data storage equipment.
  * Defense equipment and secure systems.
  * Solar panels, EV batteries, and green energy components.


### **Secure Data Destruction**for Defense and Government Needs****
For organizations dealing with sensitive or classified information, METech offers:
  * **Hard Drive Shredding** : Complete physical destruction to prevent any possibility of recovery.
  * **Certified Data Wiping** : Secure erasure for repurposed or resold devices.
  * **On-Site or Off-Site Services** : Flexible options to suit your security requirements.


All methods comply with government protocols, protecting your data and ensuring organizational privacy.
### **Compliant and Certified Recycling –**Trusted Certifications for Peace of Mind****
METech Recycling is fully certified and compliant with the highest industry standards, ensuring your e-waste is handled responsibly and securely:
  * **R2v3 Certification** : Globally recognized for responsible recycling practices.
  * **ISO 14001** : Environmental management standards.
  * **ITAR Registration** : Specialized handling of defense-related materials.
  * **NIST 800-88** : Secure media sanitization.


These certifications demonstrate our commitment to environmentally responsible practices and data security, ensuring that your organization remains compliant with all necessary regulations.
### **Partner with METech for Secure Electronics Recycling**
At METech Recycling, we combine over five decades of experience with cutting-edge certifications to deliver reliable, secure, and sustainable recycling solutions. By partnering with us, your organization can meet all compliance requirements while demonstrating a commitment to national security, environmental stewardship, and sustainability.
[Contact us today](https://www.metechrecycling.com/contact-us/) to discuss how METech can meet your electronics recycling needs!

e-Waste Recycling[admin](https://www.metechrecycling.com/author/admin/ "Posts by admin")2025-07-11T16:29:44+00:00
# e-Waste Recycling: Secure, Responsible Solutions for Your Business
At Metech Recycling, we understand that proper **e-waste recycling** is more than just good business practice—it’s essential for protecting your data, your reputation, and our environment. As an industry leader with years of experience, we provide comprehensive, certified e-waste recycling solutions tailored to businesses, government agencies, and organizations of all sizes.
Electronic waste, or e-waste, includes discarded computers, servers, monitors, mobile devices, and other electronic equipment that has reached the end of its useful life. Improper disposal of these items can lead to serious environmental hazards, data breaches, and regulatory fines. That’s why partnering with a trusted provider like Metech Recycling ensures your obsolete equipment is handled securely and responsibly, from collection to final disposition.
Our end-to-end **e-waste recycling** process starts with secure collection and transportation of your retired electronics. We adhere to the strictest industry standards, maintaining full chain-of-custody documentation and offering services like asset tracking, certified data destruction, and environmentally responsible material recovery. Our R2v3 certification and other industry accreditations demonstrate our commitment to best practices and sustainability.
When you choose Metech Recycling, you’re choosing more than compliance—you’re choosing peace of mind. Our experienced team will work with you to develop a customized recycling plan that fits your operational needs and sustainability goals. Whether you have a few outdated computers or an entire data center to decommission, you can count on us to help you meet your ESG objectives and reduce your environmental footprint.
Additionally, our secure data destruction services ensure that all sensitive information is permanently destroyed, protecting your business from costly data leaks. We offer both physical destruction and software-based data eradication, providing you with certificates of destruction for your records.
Ready to make a difference with responsible **e-waste recycling**? Join the many businesses and organizations that trust Metech Recycling to handle their end-of-life electronics safely, securely, and sustainably. Contact us today to learn more about our services or to schedule a pickup.
## Request a [Free e-Waste Recycling Quote](https://www.metechrecycling.com/contact-us/)
### Accepted Materials
Category | Accepted Items  
---|---  
Electronics & IT Equipment | 
  * Computers (Desktops, Laptops, Servers, Mainframes, ITAD equipment)
  * Hard Drives & SSDs (Data Destruction available)
  * Networking Equipment (Routers, Switches, Modems, Telecom Equipment)
  * Monitors (LCD, LED, CRT – restrictions may apply)
  * Peripherals (Keyboards, Mice, etc.)
  * Office Electronics (Printers, Scanners, Copiers, Fax Machines, Laser
  * Scanners, Calculators, Telephones, Multi-Function Devices)

  
Consumer & Household Electronics | 
  * Televisions (LCD, LED, Projection; Plasma models may have restrictions)
  * Cable Boxes & Satellite Receivers – DVD Players, VCRs, CD Players
  * Audio/Visual Equipment (Speakers, Stereos, Projectors)
  * Gaming/Video Game Consoles and Accessories
  * Digital Cameras & Camcorders – Electric Fans, Vacuum Cleaners, Stereo Equipment
  * Small Kitchen Appliances (mixers, toasters, etc.)
  * Mobile Devices (Tablets, Smartphones; batteries removed where applicable)

  
Battery & Energy Storage Systems | 
  * Lithium-ion Batteries (EV, UPS, Industrial)
  * Lead-Acid Batteries (Sealed & Flooded)
  * NiCd & NiMH Batteries
  * Alkaline Batteries (Bulk quantities preferred)
  * Uninterruptible Power Supply (UPS) Systems
  * Battery Energy Storage Systems (BESS)

  
Renewable Energy & Power Equipment | 
  * Solar Panels (Working & Non-Working)
  * Inverters & Power Converters
  * Wind Turbine Electronics & Components
  * Transformers, Capacitors, Circuit Breakers

  
Telecom & Data Center Equipment | 
  * Phone Systems (VoIP & Landline)
  * Fiber Optic & Copper Cables
  * Data Center Racks & PDUs
  * Enterprise Server Equipment

  
Display Technologies | 
  * CRT Monitors & TVs
  * LCD, OLED, LED, Plasma Televisions and monitors

  
Industrial & Manufacturing Electronics | 
  * Robotics and Automated Equipment
  * PLCs, Motor Drives, Control Boards
  * Test and Measurement Equipment
  * Electric Motors, Generators, Power Supplies

  
Miscellaneous Materials | 
  * Medical Electronics (Non-Biohazardous)
  * Electric Vehicle (EV) Chargers and Components
  * Scrap Circuit Boards (Precious Metal Recovery available)
  * Cables, Wiring, and Connectors

  
### Non-Acceptable Items
Category | Non-Acceptable Items  
---|---  
Hazardous & Radioactive Materials | 
  * Radioactive Devices
  * Hazardous Waste
  * Bio-Hazard Items (medical test kits, syringes, medical wastes, adult toys)
  * Hazardous Household Waste (pesticides, paint, used oil, cleaning supplies)

  
Fluorescent & Mercury Items | 
  * Broken Fluorescent Bulbs (unless properly packaged)
  * Mercury-Containing Items (electric irons, thermostats, switches, smoke detectors, exit signs, broken lamps)

  
Battery Concerns | 
  * Loose or Damaged Batteries (burnt, bulging, leaking)

  
Other Items | 
  * Pressurized Containers (fire extinguishers, propane/butane canisters)
  * Non-Electronic Waste (items lacking both a circuit board and a power cord)
  * Large Household Appliances (refrigerators, washers, dryers, ovens, water heaters, water coolers, air conditioners, space heaters)
  * Trash/Food Waste/Garbage/Green Waste

Electronics Recycling[admin](https://www.metechrecycling.com/author/admin/ "Posts by admin")2025-05-05T12:31:40+00:00
# Electronics Recycling
### METech is a Premier Electronics Recycling Resource
Finding an electronics recycling resource to responsibly recycle a wide range of electronics can be challenging. From standard business and IT equipment, to biotech, medical devices and consumer electronics recycling, we can help. METech Recycling invests in the labor-intensive process of disassembling and separating electronic devices into four distinct material streams: precious metals, other metals, plastics, and glass, prior to utilizing our in-house mechanical shredding capabilities to further reduce the commodities particulate size before smelting and reintroduction into new manufacturing – a complete cradle to cradle approach! Examples of the range of products we de-manufacture, shred and recycle responsibly include consumer electronics, outdated telecom, data center & medical equipment, as well as all computer products — virtually anything with a circuit board! METech Recycling’s facilities efficiently process millions of pounds of electronic equipment while providing detailed tracking and reporting for clients.
METech Recycling is your partner in demonstrating sustainable business practices and avoiding environmental and professional liability. we customize electronics recycling, inventory management and disposal solutions to meet your needs. Electronics recycling is serious business and clients benefit from our transparent tracking and audit processes for commodity recovery and recycling. Manufacturers, contract manufacturers, and repair centers know that occasionally products must be securely destroyed and recycled to protect brand identity or intellectual property. METech Recycling offers Secure Physical Destruction of these products, and provides documentation to keep unauthorized products from reaching secondary markets.
### Acceptable Materials
Information Technology & Data Center Equipment Servers, Switches, Routers, Telecom, Load Balancers, Firewalls, Intrusion Detection Devices, NAS/SAN Storage Systems, Enterprise Storage Systems, Hard Drives, Wireless Access Points, RF Equipment, CPU’s, LCD Monitors, Laptops, Tablets, Desktop Computers, Random Access Memory (RAM), Motherboards, VOIP Phones, Enterprise Phone Systems, I/O Cards, Host Bus Adapters, Fiber Controllers, Ethernet Controllers, Solar Panels.
📩 [Contact us today](https://www.metechrecycling.com/contact-us/) to get started with a customized IT Asset Management and Electronic Recycling solution.

![IT-Asset-Management](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/IT-Asset-Management.jpg)
IT Asset Management (ITAM/ITAD)[admin](https://www.metechrecycling.com/author/admin/ "Posts by admin")2025-05-05T14:05:39+00:00
# IT Asset Management (ITAM/ITAD)
### **Maximize Performance, Protect Value, Ensure Compliance**
[![R2 Certified](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/11/R2-Stacked-300x185.png)](https://sustainableelectronics.org/)At METech Recycling, our IT Asset Management (ITAM/ITAD) services are designed for enterprise clients looking to responsibly and profitably manage the lifecycle of their technology. As a nationally certified R2v3 Responsible Recycler, we go beyond simple asset tracking. We provide full diagnostic testing, grading, data sanitization, and refurbishment of IT equipment to ensure functionality and resale value while maintaining strict compliance standards.
### **Comprehensive Diagnostic Testing**
Every device we receive is subjected to rigorous testing using industry-grade software and procedures. This includes functionality checks, performance assessments, and a grading process that categorizes each asset by condition—enabling more accurate reporting and market positioning.
### **Data Sanitization and Risk Mitigation**
Before any asset is approved for resale or redeployment, all data is removed using NIST SP800-88-compliant processes. We also offer secure physical destruction options for storage media. Our approach eliminates data breach risks while maintaining compliance with privacy regulations like HIPAA and FACTA.
### **Recover Value Through Resale**
Once cleared of data, devices are refurbished to extend product life and maximize returns. Our in-house technicians replace defective parts, update firmware, and restore appearance and functionality to like-new condition. This not only improves market value but also supports a circular economy by reducing e-waste.
### **Customized ITAM Programs**
We tailor programs to your unique business needs. Whether you need monthly pickups from multiple locations or scheduled audits of your asset inventory, METech works as an extension of your IT and procurement teams.
### **Why IT Asset Management (ITAM/ITAD) with METech?**
  * R2v3-certified workflows
  * Transparent chain of custody
  * Secure client portal with detailed reporting
  * Optimized resale channels and return on investment


**Let us turn your retired equipment into a sustainability success story.**
📩 [Contact us today](https://www.metechrecycling.com/contact-us/) to get started with a customized IT Asset Management solution.

IT Asset Recovery[admin](https://www.metechrecycling.com/author/admin/ "Posts by admin")2025-05-05T14:32:54+00:00
# IT Asset Recovery
### **Unlock the Value of Your Retired Technology with IT Asset Recovery**
At METech Recycling, our IT Asset Recovery program empowers organizations to maximize the return on their retired, surplus, or decommissioned electronic assets. Whether you’re upgrading equipment, consolidating offices, or clearing out storage, our end-to-end recovery process ensures you extract the greatest possible value—while remaining fully compliant with environmental regulations and data security requirements. We help transform aging tech into revenue, all while keeping sustainability and accountability at the forefront.
### **Comprehensive Evaluation and Grading**
Every piece of recovered equipment is subjected to a thorough evaluation using our standardized grading system. This process includes hardware testing, cosmetic inspection, and functional diagnostics. Devices that pass these evaluations are securely sanitized using industry-standard data destruction protocols and, when feasible, refurbished to enhance resale value. Only items that meet our quality and functionality standards are forwarded to appropriate resale or redeployment channels, minimizing waste and maximizing ROI.
### **Multi-Channel Resale Strategy**
To ensure top-tier value for your assets, we leverage a diversified resale strategy. This includes trusted wholesale resellers, curated online marketplaces, and targeted auction platforms. Our internal market analytics team continuously monitors demand trends and pricing benchmarks across different device categories, helping us determine the most lucrative resale path for each asset. This approach not only optimizes financial return but also expedites asset turnover.
### **Charitable and Employee Redeployment Options**
Looking to make a positive impact? We support clients in repurposing refurbished equipment through charitable donations or employee purchase programs. Whether you’re equipping a local nonprofit or offering discounted devices to staff, we handle secure data wiping, inventory tracking, and logistics—ensuring that these alternative channels are as safe and seamless as possible.
### **Environmental Responsibility**
For devices that can’t be reused or sold, METech provides responsible end-of-life recycling that complies with the highest industry standards, including R2v3 certification. Our processes prioritize maximum material recovery while enforcing a strict zero-landfill policy, reducing environmental harm and supporting a circular economy.
### **Financial Transparency and Reporting During IT Asset Recovery**
With every asset recovery project, METech delivers a comprehensive financial breakdown. Clients receive clear reports that detail gross and net resale values, refurbishment and processing costs, logistics fees, and the final return on investment (ROI). This level of transparency ensures full accountability and helps organizations assess the true value of their recovered technology.
### Ready to get more from your IT asset lifecycle? [Let’s discuss your asset recovery goals](https://www.metechrecycling.com/contact-us/)
## Delivering Eco-Responsible Solutions
![Metech Recycling](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Metech-Footer-Logo.png)
METech Recycling holds the required R2v3 certification in addition to other voluntary certifications allowing us to complete the Circle of Excellence assuring best practices in electronics recycling.

Medical Equipment Recycling[admin](https://www.metechrecycling.com/author/admin/ "Posts by admin")2025-06-17T17:51:42+00:00
# Medical Equipment Recycling Program – Recycle Responsibly
### **Secure and Compliant Medical Equipment Recycling**
Medical equipment and devices require specialized handling due to their complexities and strict regulatory requirements, including **HIPAA compliance**. METech Recycling offers a **Medical Equipment Recycling Program** tailored to help healthcare providers, hospitals, clinics, and manufacturers responsibly manage outdated or unused medical devices.
### **Why Recycle Medical Equipment?**
Unused or obsolete medical equipment can accumulate quickly. Instead of risking improper disposal, choose a sustainable and secure alternative—recycling. METech Recycling simplifies the process, helping to prevent waste, reduce harmful emissions, and recover valuable materials for reuse, all while ensuring full compliance with environmental and data security regulations.
### **What Medical Equipment Can Be Recycled?**
Our **Medical Equipment Recycling** program accepts a wide range of devices, including:
  * Diagnostic machines
  * Robotic systems
  * Monitoring equipment
  * Imaging devices (X-ray, MRI, CT scanners)
  * Surgical tools
  * Laboratory instruments
  * Hospital beds and patient care items
  * And more!


Unsure if your equipment qualifies? Contact our team for guidance.
### **Why Choose METech Recycling![Medical Equipment Recycling](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/11/medical-equip-300x238.png)**
Since 1968, METech Recycling has been a trusted partner in the medical device field. Our **national footprint** ensures reliable service from coast to coast, and our certified recycling centers guarantee compliance with environmental regulations, data security protocols, and HIPAA standards.
### **How the Medical Equipment Recycling Program Works**
  1. **Contact Us**  
Reach out to our team to discuss your medical equipment recycling needs.
  2. **Collection**  
We arrange convenient pickup or drop-off options to suit your schedule.
  3. **Data Security**
     * We provide **certified data destruction services** for sensitive information stored on devices like imaging systems or computers.
     * Serialization, photo or video documentation of destruction, and even witness destruction services are available.
  4. **Data Reporting**
     * All data related to your recycling project is securely uploaded to your private portal, giving you 24/7 access to: 
       * Chain of custody reports
       * Data destruction certificates
       * Certificates of recycling (COD)
       * Bills of lading
       * Settlement reports, and more.
  5. **Environmentally Friendly Processing**  
We safely dismantle and recycle components, ensuring all materials are responsibly handled according to **R2v3 standards**.


### **Benefits of Recycling Medical Equipment with METech**
  * **Sustainability** : Support a circular economy by reducing the demand for new raw materials.
  * **Regulatory Compliance** : Meet all environmental and health regulations with ease.
  * **Data Protection** : Securely destroy sensitive information, protecting patient confidentiality.
  * **Convenience** : Our nationwide service makes it simple to recycle medical equipment.


### **Where to Recycle Medical Equipment?**
Are you wondering **where to recycle medical equipment**? **METech Recycling** has multiple locations nationwide, and our collection services make it simple to dispose of your old or unused devices. Reach out today to find the closest recycling center or schedule a pickup.
### **Why Partner with METech Recycling?**
  * We have been in the recycling industry since 1968.
  * Certified expertise in **secure data destruction** and **responsible recycling**.
  * Customized solutions designed for healthcare providers, hospitals, and manufacturers.
  * A steadfast commitment to protecting the environment.


### Ready to **recycle medical equipment**?
Contact METech Recycling today to learn more about our Medical Equipment Recycling Program and discover how we can help you securely and sustainably manage your devices.

Metech Carbon Footprint Calculator[admin](https://www.metechrecycling.com/author/admin/ "Posts by admin")2025-09-23T11:29:16+00:00
# Metech Carbon Footprint Calculator
Understanding your organization’s carbon footprint is the first step toward creating a more sustainable future. METech Recycling’s Carbon Footprint Calculator makes it simple for businesses to measure the environmental impact of their operations, from energy consumption to e-waste generation. By identifying your carbon footprint, you gain the insights needed to reduce emissions, improve efficiency, and meet growing environmental standards. Whether your goal is to strengthen corporate sustainability initiatives, comply with regulatory requirements, or demonstrate social responsibility to customers and stakeholders, this tool helps you make informed decisions that drive measurable impact for both your business and the planet.
**Disclaimer**  
This calculator is provided for informational purposes only. While METech Recycling has made every effort to use the most recent and reliable emissions factors and methodologies, results are estimates and may not reflect the exact carbon footprint of your specific operations. Data sources include the U.S. EPA, IPCC, and other publicly available references, but values may change over time as factors are updated. This tool does not replace a formal greenhouse gas inventory or third-party verification.
![Metech Recycling](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Metech-Footer-Logo.png)
METech Recycling holds the required R2v3 certification in addition to other voluntary certifications allowing us to complete the Circle of Excellence assuring best practices in electronics recycling.

METech Recycling Locations[admin](https://www.metechrecycling.com/author/admin/ "Posts by admin")2025-10-23T01:08:52+00:00
# All METech Recycling Locations
METech Recycling locations consists of **five R2v3 Certified recycling facilities** strategically located across the United States. Each facility is fully equipped to handle a wide range of electronics recycling and IT asset disposition (ITAD) needs, with a strong focus on environmental compliance and data security.
By placing our facilities in key regions, we’re able to provide responsive service, reduce transportation costs, and minimize environmental impact. All locations maintain the highest standards of operation, ensuring consistency in quality and compliance.
To offer nationwide coverage, METech also partners with a **select network of approved third-party providers**. These partners are thoroughly vetted to meet our rigorous operational and security standards, allowing us to extend our reach while maintaining service excellence. Whether your company has one location or hundreds across the U.S., we can build a customized solution to fit your needs.
For further information about METech Recycling Locations, please [contact us](https://www.metechrecycling.com/contact-us/).

## METech Recycling Locations Private Fleet
To better serve our clients and maintain end-to-end control of secure transport, METech operates its own **dedicated private fleet**. Our team is trained in safe handling, chain-of-custody procedures, and secure data transport protocols.
### Local Service Pick-up
  * Available within **1.5 hours** of each METech processing facility
  * Fast, secure, and cost-effective
  * Ideal for regularly scheduled or on-demand pickups


### Extended Service Pick-up
  * Available within **2.5 hours** of each facility
  * Offers the same secure transport at a slightly higher rate
  * Great for clients located just beyond our local radius


### Nationwide 3PL Support
For clients outside of local or extended coverage zones, we utilize **trusted third-party logistics (3PL) providers** to ensure safe, certified transportation to the nearest METech facility. Our team coordinates all logistics to make the process seamless and compliant.
![Metech Recycling](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Metech-Footer-Logo.png)
METech Recycling holds the required R2v3 certification in addition to other voluntary certifications allowing us to complete the Circle of Excellence assuring best practices in electronics recycling.

OEM Recycling[admin](https://www.metechrecycling.com/author/admin/ "Posts by admin")2025-06-17T17:53:10+00:00
#  **OEM Recycling Solutions –****Maximize Value and Sustainability**
### **Maximize Value and Sustainability with OEM Recycling Solutions**
In today’s fast-paced manufacturing world, **Original Equipment Manufacturers (OEMs)** face increasing pressure to meet sustainability goals while managing complex waste streams. **METech Recycling** provides innovative and comprehensive **OEM recycling solutions** that help manufacturers responsibly recycle outdated, defective, or end-of-life equipment, ensuring maximum value recovery and environmental compliance.
### **Innovative Recycling for Cutting-Edge OEM Equipment**
As a leader in **OEM recycling** , **METech Recycling** utilizes advanced technology to process a wide range of materials, including electronics, metals, plastics, and hazardous components. Our services are tailored to support the specific needs of OEMs, ensuring that your old or obsolete equipment is recycled in an environmentally responsible way. With a focus on recovering valuable materials, we help minimize waste and maximize resource efficiency.
### **Partner with METech for Comprehensive OEM Recycling Services**
At **METech Recycling** , we understand the unique challenges that OEMs face when it comes to disposing of equipment responsibly. By partnering with us, you can access:
  * **Customized Recycling Solutions** : Tailored services to meet the specific recycling requirements of your OEM equipment.
  * **Secure Data Destruction** : Certified destruction of sensitive data from electronic devices to protect your business and clients.
  * **Compliance with Regulations** : Full adherence to environmental laws and industry regulations, ensuring your recycling practices meet or exceed standards.
  * **Resource Recovery** : Recovered materials can be reused in new manufacturing, reducing the need for virgin raw materials and lowering production costs.


### **Why OEM Recycling is Essential**
With rapid advancements in technology, OEM equipment often becomes obsolete before it reaches the end of its functional life. Recycling this equipment is essential for several reasons:
  * **Environmental Protection** : Recycling helps prevent harmful materials from entering the environment.
  * **Cost Efficiency** : Recovering valuable components from recycled equipment reduces the need for new raw materials.
  * **Sustainability Goals** : Recycling supports your company’s sustainability initiatives and improves your brand’s reputation.
  * **Regulatory Compliance** : Recycling ensures that your business meets government and industry regulations for equipment disposal.


### **OEM Recycling Process**
Our **OEM recycling** process is designed for efficiency and sustainability:
  * **Collection** : We arrange for the pickup or drop-off of your obsolete OEM equipment.
  * **Evaluation and Sorting** : Equipment is evaluated for possible reuse, refurbishment, or recycling. Materials such as metals, plastics, and hazardous components are sorted.
  * **Data Security** : Any equipment containing sensitive data is securely wiped or destroyed.
  * **Processing and Recycling** : Equipment is dismantled, and valuable materials are recovered for reuse.
  * **Final Disposal** : Any remaining materials are disposed of safely, with full compliance to environmental regulations.
  * **Data Reporting**


All data related to your recycling project is securely uploaded to your private portal, giving you 24/7 access to:
  *     1. Chain of custody reports
    2. Data destruction certificates
    3. Certificates of recycling (COD)
    4. Bills of lading
    5. Settlement reports, and more.


### **Industries We Serve**
**METech Recycling** serves a wide range of industries, including:
  * Electronics and technology manufacturing
  * Renewable energy solutions
  * Automotive and transportation
  * Medical and healthcare equipment manufacturing
  * Industrial machinery
  * Aerospace and defense


Whether you’re managing the disposal of outdated electronics, large machinery, or medical devices, **METech Recycling** offers the expertise and facilities to handle your OEM recycling needs.
### **Maximize Sustainability and Value**
When you choose **METech Recycling** as your OEM recycling partner, you’re not just disposing of equipment—you’re contributing to a sustainable future. Our **OEM recycling solutions** are designed to:
  * Minimize waste and reduce environmental impact
  * Maximize material recovery for reuse in manufacturing
  * Ensure regulatory compliance
  * Protect sensitive data


### **Partner with METech for Comprehensive OEM Recycling Services**
From electronics, robotics, medical devices, industrial equipment, **METech Recycling** provides industry-leading **OEM recycling services** that meet your specific needs. By partnering with us, you’ll gain access to a trusted provider with over 50 years of experience in environmentally responsible recycling.
Let’s work together to create a more sustainable future. [**Contact METech Recycling**](https://www.metechrecycling.com/contact-us/) today to learn more about our **OEM recycling solutions** and how we can help your company reduce waste, recover value, and stay compliant with regulations.
[![R2 V3 Certified](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/11/R2-Stacked-300x185.png)](https://sustainableelectronics.org/)
