Our History[admin](https://www.metechrecycling.com/author/admin/ "Posts by admin")2025-11-13T17:03:51+00:00
# Our History
METech Recycling, Inc. has been in business since 1875 and is headquartered in Gilroy, California. The company was founded to recycle precious metal scrap then evolved to recycle electronic components and manufacturing by-products. Over the years, end-of-life electronic equipment, brand, proprietary design, HIPAA and all government compliance protection, secure data destruction and asset management have become the core focus as the business landscape continues to change.
[![](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Mapelville-RI-1.jpg)](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Mapelville-RI-1.jpg)
[![](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Mapelville-RI-2-1.jpg)](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Mapelville-RI-2-1.jpg)
[![](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Refinemet-HQ-Woonsocket-RI-1.jpg)](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Refinemet-HQ-Woonsocket-RI-1.jpg)
[![](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ssf_001_457-1.jpg)](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/ssf_001_457-1.jpg)
### Metech History Timeline
**1875**  
The Wildberg Brothers facility, (aka Boliden Metech) was a metal reclamation plant which operated in San Francisco between 1907 and 1986. The site was approximately 5 1/2 acres in size. This facility was used as an antimony smelting plant which operated for an unknown duration beginning in 1875.
**1907**  
The Site was purchased in 1907 by the Wildberg Brothers Company who operated a metal reclamation facility. The operations included milling, sampling, assaying of scrap materials, electrolytic deposition of silver, stripping of gold, and copper concentration. Gold, platinum, palladium, silver and copper were recovered as finished products.
**1968**  
RMI traces its origin back to 1968 in Woonsocket, R.I. At that time, Refinemet focused on precious metals and tantalum recovery. Refinemet expanded into electronics recycling by “default” in the late ’70s and early ’80s because customers like AT&T, Burroughs, DEC and IBM had large pieces of equipment that they were retiring.
**1980**  
Wildberg Brothers sold the facility to Refinemet International (RMI) in 1980. RMI primarily used the facility for precious metal scrap processing and refining.
**1983**  
In 1983, shortly after expanding into processing end-of-life electronics, Boliden, a smelting and mining company based in Stockholm, Sweden, purchased RMI and renamed it Boliden Metech. It was during this time that Metech moved the East Coast operation from Woonsocket, RI to Mapleville, RI.  
Boliden used the San Francisco facility primarily for precious metal scrap processing but did not engage in refining operations at the Site. Operations conducted onsite consisted of material sorting, sampling, and assaying before the materials were containerized for shipment to Boliden facilities overseas for processing.
**1986**  
Boliden discontinued all operations at the San Francisco site in May 1986. All buildings at the site, with the exception of Building 1, the Office Building, Building 2, the Laboratory; and Buildings 11-12, the Melt Shop, and Mechanical Processing area, were demolished and the business was moved to our current location in Gilroy, CA. Trelleborg, (the parent company of Boliden), later spun off the smelting operations under the name Boliden but retained Metech as a recycling and processing operation.  
In 2002 Viking Investment and Asset Management, based in Johannesburg, South Africa, bought Metech.
**2005**  
In 2005 Metech was acquired by MTI Corp and relocated the corporate offices from Mapleville, RI to Worcester, Mass. The company designed a processing line to include shredders and downstream separation equipment.  
At this time, Metech also discontinued receiving precious-metals-containing hazardous waste and scaled back its other local precious metals refining businesses that were not adding value to the company’s focus on integrated electronics recycling.
**2007**  
In 2007 Metech was acquired by “Centillion Environment and Recycling Ltd” of Singapore.  
In 2008 Centillion purchases “Guaranteed Recycling Xperts” (GRX) with locations in Denver, CO, Salt Lake City, UT and Omaha, NE.
**2009**  
2009 Centillion merges Metech and GRX under the Metech Recycling banner.  
In 2012 Centillion was renamed Metech International
**2016**  
In 2016 the Worcester facility was relocated once more to its current location in nearby Clinton, MA. At this time, corporate operations were permanently transferred to the Gilroy, CA facility.
**2018**  
In 2018 Metech Recycling was purchased by First America Metals Group and taken Private.
**2021**  
METech continues operating today with a strong national footprint serving industries such as medical, military, government, education, manufacturing and more. METech understands that very organization has different requirements and goals they want to accomplish for their environmental sustainability and recycling program. Therefore, off the shelf solutions can only go so far.
METech Recycling works directly with you to customize solutions that make your goals come to fruition. The results not only contribute to meeting your environmental goals, our program fosters a positive public viewpoint on your organization while promoting real actions being taken that make a difference. These programs will help protect your brand identity and security while maintaining your regulatory compliance.
Let’s work together and develop a recycling solution for your organization. Connect with us today!
![Metech Recycling](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Metech-Footer-Logo.png)
METech Recycling holds the required R2v3 certification in addition to other voluntary certifications allowing us to complete the Circle of Excellence assuring best practices in electronics recycling.

# Reporting & Client Portal Access
**Transparent, Detailed, and Accessible Anytime**
In the world of IT asset disposition and recycling, accountability and reporting are everything. METech Recycling offers enterprise-grade reporting tools and a secure online portal that gives our clients total visibility into the lifecycle of their assets.
### **Full Lifecycle Audit Reports**
Each inbound load is processed with a detailed audit that includes:
  * Order and receipt information
  * Location tracking
  * Photos
  * Asset tag, serial, and model numbers
  * Manufacturer and product specifications
  * Functionality test results and grades
  * Applied data destruction methods
  * Processing, refurbishment, and fee breakdowns


### **Custom Reporting Formats**
We tailor reporting based on your internal compliance or audit requirements. Whether you’re tracking environmental KPIs, financial returns, or chain-of-custody logs, our reports make it easy.
### **Secure Client Portal Access**
Through our web-based portal, clients can:
  * View and download real-time reports
  * Track assets by location, batch, or status
  * Monitor data destruction logs
  * Access historical project data


Our portal is user-friendly, password-protected, and accessible 24/7.
Get better insights from your recycling program. [Schedule a demo](https://www.metechrecycling.com/contact-us/) of our Client Reporting Portal today.
## Delivering Eco-Responsible Solutions

Reverse Logistics and Redeployment[admin](https://www.metechrecycling.com/author/admin/ "Posts by admin")2025-05-05T16:40:00+00:00
# **Reverse Logistics and Redeployment**
### **Streamlined Asset Return and Redistribution**
Efficient reverse logistics and redeployment is essential for any organization managing a fleet of IT assets across multiple locations. METech Recycling provides a full suite of services to recover, store, and redeploy electronics with minimal disruption to your operations.
### **Secure Asset Return**
We manage the entire return process—from on-site pickups to inventory logging at our secured facilities. All items are tracked and documented to maintain full visibility and ensure nothing is lost in transit.
### **Climate-Controlled, Monitored Storage**
Whether you’re awaiting approval on disposition or holding equipment for future redeployment, our storage facilities feature 24/7 CCTV monitoring and controlled access protocols. Devices are organized, tagged, and securely stored.
### **Flexible Redeployment Support**
Redeploying equipment internally? We’ll inventory and track assets as they move between departments, offices, or data centers. Need reimaging, refurbishment, or upgrades before redeployment? We’ve got you covered.
### **Customized Logistics Solutions**
  * Scheduled or on-demand pickups
  * Serialized inventory reports
  * Packing and kitting support
  * Onsite or offsite warehousing


Whether you’re consolidating, upgrading, or relocating, METech makes the process seamless.
Get Reverse Logistics & Redeployment services that scale with your enterprise. [Request a customized quote](https://www.metechrecycling.com/contact-us/).

Services[admin](https://www.metechrecycling.com/author/admin/ "Posts by admin")2025-07-07T13:44:27+00:00
# Services
[](https://www.metechrecycling.com/it-asset-management-itam-itad/)
## IT Asset Management
As a national R2v3 Responsible Recycler, our in-house ITAM Service professionals are required to fully test all equipment prior to resale. All clients’ assets will undergo full system diagnostic testing for functionality, grade, sanitized as well as eradicate all client data present mitigating risks. Then all the assets will be fully refurbished and properly prepared for resale.
[Learn More](https://www.metechrecycling.com/it-asset-management-itam-itad/)
[](https://www.metechrecycling.com/data-security-2/)
## Data Security
METech Recycling offers single, 3 or 7-pass software data destruction services. All data containing devices are sanitized to National Institute of Standards and Technology (NIST) SP800-88 and Department of Defense (DoD) 5220.22-M data erasure standards and are physically tracked from receipt to final disposition. Data containing devices that fail to boot, mount, detect, or are otherwise inaccessible are physically destroyed using our in-house shredding capabilities. A Certificate of Data Destruction is provided for all software data eradication and/or physical destruction jobs. This entire process also ensures compliance with both FACTA and HIPAA regulations
[Learn More](https://www.metechrecycling.com/data-security-2/)
[](https://www.metechrecycling.com/reverse-logistics-and-redeployment/)
## Reverse Logistics & Redeployment
Fully functional finished goods and/or harvested parts are inventoried and stored in a clean and secure CCTV protected environment until they are picked, packaged, and shipped.
If your organization has limited warehouse space or if you are undecided on what to do with your retired assets or perhaps you need to track and manage redeployment of assets elsewhere, we can help. METech Recycling ITAM Services can provide storage, reverse logistics, and redeployment services catered specifically to your requirements.
[Learn More](https://www.metechrecycling.com/reverse-logistics-and-redeployment/)
## IT Asset Recovery
Each fully tested and refurbished client asset can be made available for resale into secondary markets, redeployment, charitable donations or “employee-share” programs. METech Recycling ITAM Services will assist you in finding the right fit for your retired assets. Utilizing several channels and methods we ensure our clients the highest return for their retired, overstock, and end-of-life electronics.
[Learn More](https://www.metechrecycling.com/it-asset-recovery/)
## Reporting & Client Portal Access
METech provides a full audit report for each inbound load of client materials. Our audit reports contain extremely detailed, itemized, asset specific details such as: order number, order receipt date, serial number, asset tag number, manufacturer, model/part number, product type, technical specifications, test results, known failures and/or issues, equipment grade, applicable processing, test and refurbishment fees, and financial disclosure. Our clients can opt to receive our reporting by mail, email, or by using our Online Client Reporting Portal. It’s that easy!
[Learn More](https://www.metechrecycling.com/reporting-and-client-portal/)
## Data Center Solutions
At METech, we specialize in comprehensive data center solutions tailored to meet the evolving needs of your business. Our expert team is equipped to handle every aspect of your data center management, including on-site decommissioning, upgrades, and the responsible disposition of equipment. We provide meticulous inventory services complete with detailed documentation to aid in auditing and compliance, as well as optimize your opportunities for remarketing. Our R2v3 certification ensures we adhere to the highest security and environmental standards in the industry. We maintain a secure chain of custody and implement close monitoring systems to prevent any data breaches or theft.
[Learn More](https://www.metechrecycling.com/data-center-solutions/)
![Metech Recycling](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Metech-Footer-Logo.png)
METech Recycling holds the required R2v3 certification in addition to other voluntary certifications allowing us to complete the Circle of Excellence assuring best practices in electronics recycling.

Solar Panel Recycling[admin](https://www.metechrecycling.com/author/admin/ "Posts by admin")2025-08-13T16:59:44+00:00
#  **Renewable Energy Recycling –****Solar Panel Recycling**
## **Sustainable Disposal for a Greener Future**
### **Solar Panel Recycling: A Sustainable Solution for Renewable Energy**
From solar panels, inverters, transformers to BESS (battery energy storage units) and metal scrap, your renewable energy site deserves a compelling sustainability story—and METech Recycling is here to help you tell it! As solar energy continues to power the world, the need for responsible disposal of old or damaged solar panels grows. METech Recycling offers comprehensive Solar Panel Recycling services that minimize environmental impact, recover valuable materials, and uphold our **zero-landfill policy.**
### **Are Solar Panels Recyclable? Absolutely!**
Solar panels are highly recyclable, with components like glass, silicon, and metals that can be repurposed. At METech Recycling, we ensure every part of your old solar panels is processed safely, helping to reduce landfill waste and support a circular economy.
### **Why Recycle Solar Panels?**
Solar panels typically last 25-30 years before they become inefficient or damaged. Recycling them is critical to:
  * **Preventing Environmental Harm** : Proper recycling keeps hazardous materials like cadmium and lead out of the ecosystem.
  * **Recovering Valuable Resources** : Materials such as glass, silicon, and metals can be reused in new solar panels or other products.
  * **Maintaining Sustainability** : Recycling aligns with renewable energy’s mission to protect the environment.


### **Why METech is a Leader in Solar Panel Recycling**
As a trusted partner for businesses, individuals, solar energy providers, and installers, METech Recycling combines advanced recycling techniques with an unwavering commitment to sustainability.
### **How Does Solar Panel Recycling Work?**
Our efficient process ensures maximum material recovery and minimal environmental impact:
  1. **Collection** : We provide flexible options for pickup or drop-off.
  2. **Disassembly** : Panels are carefully dismantled to separate materials like glass, silicon, and metals.
  3. **Material Recovery** : Valuable resources are processed for reuse in new products.
  4. **Safe Disposal** : Hazardous materials are handled in compliance with environmental regulations.


### **Benefits of Recycling Solar Panels**
  * **Environmental Impact** : Recycling reduces the need for raw material extraction and diverts waste from landfills.
  * **Resource Recovery** : Extracted materials are reused in various industries, supporting sustainability.
  * **Regulatory Compliance** : Our services meet strict environmental regulations, ensuring safe handling of hazardous materials.
  * **Cost-Efficiency** : Recycling helps lower waste management costs for businesses.
  * **Sustainability Continuity** : Renewable energy’s green promise extends to the end of your panels’ life cycle, maintaining your sustainability story.


### **Why Choose METech Recycling?**
  * **50+ Years of Expertise** : A trusted name in the recycling industry.
  * **Cutting-Edge Technology** : Advanced solutions for solar panel recycling.
  * **Zero-Landfill Commitment** : Responsible and eco-friendly practices.
  * **Custom Solutions** : Tailored services for solar energy providers, installers, and manufacturers.


By partnering with METech Recycling, you ensure your old solar panels are handled responsibly, contributing to a greener future while maximizing your solar investments.
### **Recycle Solar Panels with Confidence**
Looking for a reliable solar recycling partner? METech Recycling offers **state-of-the-art, environmentally responsible solutions** for your renewable energy needs. Join us in creating a sustainable legacy by giving your solar panels a second life.
**Contact us today** to learn more about our Solar Recycling Program and keep your green energy story thriving from start to finish.
[![R2 V3 Certified](https://www.metechrecycling.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/11/R2-Stacked-300x185.png)](https://sustainableelectronics.org/)
